                       Send messages that students and parents
                       <span class="Text Text-module--this---highlight--2-r5D Text-module--this---noWrap--IWrfR">
                        can't miss.
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </h1>
                   <div class="Title--subtext Title-module--subtext--61trJ">
                    <span class="Text">
                     <div class="Text Copy Copy---none">
                      <p>
                       Teaching is about your students, not tracking down handouts or playing phone tag. Remind makes it easy to reach the people you need to reach.
                      </p>
                     </div>
                    </span>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                 </header>
                 <div class="Container Container-module--this--4JkHs Container-module--this---left--57gcF Container-module--this---flush--1r-i1 Container-module--this---xsmall--3wymR Module1-module--actions--MPG7N">
                  <div class="Buttons Buttons-module--this--hOB2X">
                   <div class="Buttons--item Buttons-module--item--BDEOG">
                    <a class="LinkBase Link Link-module--this--3CGQ5 Link-module--this---brand--18aay Button Button-module--this--1yxKG Button-module--this---brand--1shar Button-module--this---primary--1uaXr" href="/teachers/">
                     Learn more
                    </a>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                </div>
               </div>
              </div>
             </div>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>

                   <h2 class="Heading Title-module--small--1xAAf Heading-module--this---4--Noge4">
                    For families
